be in one state at a time\n   118→     * The expected state transitions with the following defined states is:\n   119→     *\n   120→     * <pre>\n   121→     *                 +-------------+\n   122→     *          +<---- | Created (0) |\n   123→     *          |      +-----+-------+\n   124→     *          |            |\n   125→     *          |            v\n   126→     *          |      +-----+-------+\n   127→     *          +<---- | Starting (1)|----->+\n   128→     *          |      +-----+-------+      |\n   129→     *          |                           |\n   130→     *          |            +<----------+  |\n   131→     *          |            |           |  |\n   132→     *          |            v           |  |\n   133→     *          |      +-----+-------+   |  |\n   134→     *          +<---- | Partitions  | --+  |\n   135→     *          |      | Revoked (2) | <----+\n   136→     *          |      +-----+-------+      |\n   137→     *          |           |  ^    | Assigned (3)| <----+\n   142→     *          |      +-----+-------+      |\n   143→     *          |            |              |\n   144→     *          |            +<----------+  |\n   145→     *          |            |           |  |\n   146→     *          |            v           |  |\n   147→     *          |      +-----+-------+   |  |\n   148→     *          |      |             | --+  |\n   149→     *          |      | Running (4) | ---->+\n   150→     *          |      +-----+-------+\n   151→     *          |            |\n   152→     *          |            v\n   153→     *          |      +-----+-------+\n   154→     *          +----> | Pending     |\n   155→     *                 | Shutdown (5)|\n   156→     *                 +-----+-------+\n   157→     *                       |\n   158→     *                       v\n   159→     *                 +-----+-------+\n   160→     *                 | Dead (6)    |\n   161→     *                 +-------------+\n   162→     * </pre>\n   163→     *\n   164→     * Note the following:\n   165→     * <ul>\n   166→     *     <li>Any state can go to PENDING_SHUTDOWN. That is because streams can be closed at any time.</li>\n   167→     *     <li>\n   168→     *         State PENDING_SHUTDOWN may want to transit to some other states other than DEAD,\n   169→     *         in the corner case when the shutdown is triggered while the thread is still in the rebalance loop.\n   170→     *         In this case we will forbid the transition but will not treat as an error.\n   171→     *     </li>\n   172→     *     <li>\n   173→     *         State PARTITIONS_REVOKED may want transit to itself indefinitely, in the corner case when\n   174→     *         the coordinator repeatedly fails in-between revoking partitions and assigning new partitions.\n   175→     *         Also during streams instance start up PARTITIONS_REVOKED may want to transit to itself as well.\n   176→     *         In this case we will allow the transition but it will be a no-op as the set of revoked partitions\n   177→     *         should be empty.\n   178→     *     </li>\n   179→     * </ul>\n   180→     */\n   181→    public enum State implements ThreadStateTransitionValidator {\n   182→\n   183→        CREATED(1, 5),                    // 0\n   184→        STARTING(2, 3, 5),                // 1\n   185→        PARTITIONS_REVOKED(2, 3, 5),      // 2\n   186→        PARTITIONS_ASSIGNED(2, 3, 4, 5),  // 3\n   187→        RUNNING(2, 3, 4, 5),              // 4\n   188→        PENDING_SHUTDOWN(6),              // 5\n   189→        DEAD; org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.internals.TopologyMetadata.UNNAMED_TOPOLOGY;\n   119→\n   120→/**\n   121→ * A Kafka client that allows for performing continuous computation on input coming from one or more input topics and\n   122→ * sends output to zero, one, or more output topics.\n   123→ * <p>\n   124→ * The computational logic can be specified either by using the {@link Topology} to define a DAG topology of\n   125→ * {@link org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.api.Processor}s or by using the {@link StreamsBuilder} which provides the high-level DSL to define\n   126→ * transformations.\n   127→ * <p>\n   128→ * One {@code KafkaStreams} instance can contain one or more threads specified in the configs for the processing work.\n   129→ * <p>\n   130→ * A {@code KafkaStreams} instance can co-ordinate with any other instances with the same\n   131→ * {@link StreamsConfig#APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG application ID} (whether in the same process, on other processes on this\n   132→ * machine, or on remote machines) as a single (possibly distributed) stream processing application.\n   133→ * These instances will divide up the work based on the assignment of the input topic partitions so that all partitions\n   134→ * are being consumed.\n   135→ * If instances are added or fail, all (remaining) instances will rebalance the partition assignment among themselves\n   136→ * to balance processing load and ensure that all input topic partitions are processed.\n   137→ * <p>\n   138→ * Internally a {@code KafkaStreams} instance contains a normal {@link KafkaProducer} and {@link KafkaConsumer} instance\n   139→ * that is used for reading input and writing output.\n   140→ * <p>\n   141→ * A simple example might look like this:\n   142→ * <pre>{@code\n   143→ * Properties props = new Properties();\n   144→ * props.put(StreamsConfig.APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG, \"my-stream-processing-application\");\n   145→ * props.put(StreamsConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, \"localhost:9092\");\n   146→ * props.put(StreamsConfig.DEFAULT_KEY_SERDE_CLASS_CONFIG, Serdes.String().getClass());\n   147→ * props.put(StreamsConfig.DEFAULT_VALUE_SERDE_CLASS_CONFIG, Serdes.String().getClass());\n   148→ *\n   149→ * StreamsBuilder builder = new StreamsBuilder();\n   150→ * builder.<String, String>stream(\"my-input-topic\").mapValues(value -> String.valueOf(value.length())).to(\"my-output-topic\");\n   151→ *\n   152→ * KafkaStreams streams = new KafkaStreams(builder.build(), props);\n   153→ * streams.start();\n   154→ * }</pre>\n   155→ *\n   156→ * @see org.apache.kafka.streams.StreamsBuilder\n   157→ * @see org.apache.kafka.streams.Topology\n   158→ */\n   159→public class KafkaStreams implements AutoCloseable {\n   160→\n   161→    private static final String JMX_PREFIX = \"kafka.streams\";\n   162→\n   163→    // processId is expected to be unique across JVMs and to 176→    protected final Admin adminClient;\n   177→    private final StreamsMetricsImpl streamsMetrics;\n   178→    private final long totalCacheSize;\n   179→    private final StreamStateListener streamStateListener;\n   180→    private final DelegatingStateRestoreListener delegatingStateRestoreListener;\n   181→    private final UUID processId;\n   182→    private final KafkaClientSupplier DelegatingStandbyUpdateListener delegatingStandbyUpdateListener;\n   186→    private final LogContext logContext;\n   187→\n   188→    GlobalStreamThread globalStreamThread;\n   189→    protected StateDirectory stateDirectory = null;\n   190→    private KafkaStreams.StateListener stateListener;\n   191→    private BiConsumer<Throwable, Boolean> streamsUncaughtExceptionHandler;\n   192→ the ReentrantLock allows the same thread to acquire it multiple times, the problem is that `wakeupThreads()` is a PUBLIC method that other code paths might call directly while holding OTHER locks, creating deadlock scenarios.\n\n### **CRITICAL DEADLOCK #2: Lock Ordering Inversion Between topologyLock and TaskManager Locks**\n\n**Files:**\n- lock (topologyLock) from the same thread during the lambda execution could cause issues if `createPendingTasks()` or `maybeCloseTasksFromRemovedTopologies()` try to acquire it indirectly.\n\n### **CRITICAL DEADLOCK #3: Cross-Lock Ordering Between StreamThread.stateLock and TopologyMetadata.topologyLock**\n\n**Files:**\n- `/app/streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/internals/StreamThread.java` (lines 1414-1425)\n- `/app/streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/KafkaStreams.java` (lines }\n}\n```\n\n**Path C (StateListener callback - StateListener.onChange):**\n```\npublic synchronized void onChange(...) {  // line 649\n    // This is called from KafkaStreams.setState()\n    // While stateLock is held\n    registerStreamThread()  // line 678\n}\n```\n\n**The Deadlock Scenario:**\n\n1. **Thread A (Main/NamedTopology thread):**\n   - Calls `topologyMetadata.registerAndBuildNewTopology()`\n   - Acquires `topologyLock`\n   - Calls `wakeupThreads()` → signals `topologyCV`\n   - Wakes up StreamThreads waiting in `maybeWaitForNonEmptyTopology()`\n\n2. **Thread B (StreamThread1):**\n   - Calls `checkForTopologyUpdates()`\n   - Calls `maybeWaitForNonEmptyTopology()`\n   - Acquires `topologyLock` and waits on `topologyCV.await()`\n   - Gets signalled and wakes up\n   - Needs to exit the await loop\n   - But if another thread tries to access `topologyLock` and holds `stateLock`, DEADLOCK\n\n3. **Thread C (Another StreamThread or main thread):**\n   - Tries to call `waitOnThreadState()` in StreamThread\n   - Acquires `StreamThread.stateLock`\n   - Tries to access topologyMetadata information\n   - Waiting for `topologyLock` which Thread B might hold\n   - Meanwhile Thread B is waiting for something that requires `stateLock`\n   - **DEADLOCK**\n\n### **Key Files with Locking Issues:**\n\n| File builder.allSourcePatternStrings();\n   331→\n   332→        final Set<String> newInputTopics = new HashSet<>(inputTopics);\n   333→        newInputTopics.addAll(inputPatterns);\n   334→\n   335→        final int numNewInputTopics = newInputTopics.size();\n   336→        allInputTopicsCopy.addAll(newInputTopics);\n   337→\n   338→        if (allInputTopicsCopy.size() != numInputTopics + numNewInputTopics) {\n   339→            inputTopics.retainAll(allInputTopicsCopy);\n   340→            inputPatterns.retainAll(allInputTopicsCopy);\n   341→            log.error(\"Tried to add the NamedTopology {} but it had overlap with other input topics {} or patterns {}\",\n   342→                      builder.topologyName(), inputTopics, inputPatterns);\n   343→            throw new TopologyException(\"Named Topologies may not subscribe to the same input topics or patterns\");\n   344→        }\n   345→\n   346→        final ProcessorTopology globalTopology = builder.buildGlobalStateTopology();\n   347→        if (globalTopology != null) {\n   348→            if (builder.topologyName() != null) {\n   349→                throw new IllegalStateException(\"Global state stores are not supported with Named Topologies\");\n   350→            } else if (this.globalTopology != null) {\n   351→                throw new TopologyException(\"Topology builder had global state, but global topology has already been set\");\n   352→            } else {\n   353→                this.globalTopology = globalTopology;\n   354→                globalStateStores.putAll(builder.globalStateStores());\n   355→            }\n   356→        }\n   357→        allInputTopics.addAll(newInputTopics);\n   358→    }\n   359→\n   360→    public int numStreamThreads(final StreamsConfig config) {\n   361→        final int configuredNumStreamThreads = config.getInt(StreamsConfig.NUM_STREAM_THREADS_CONFIG);\n   362→\n   363→        // If there are named topologies but some are empty, this indicates a bug in user code\n   364→        if (hasNamedTopologies()) {\n   365→            if (hasNoLocalTopology()) {\n   366→                log.error(\"Detected a named topology with no input topics, a named topology may not be empty.\");\n   367→                throw new TopologyException(\"Topology has no stream threads and no global threads, \" +\n   368→                                                \"must subscribe to at least one source topic or pattern.\");\n   369→            }\n   370→        } else {\n   371→            // If both the global and non-global topologies are empty, this indicates a bug in user code\n   372→            if (hasNoLocalTopology() && !hasGlobalTopology()) {\n   373→                log.error(\"Topology with no input topics will create no stream threads and no global thread.\");\n   374→                throw new TopologyException(\"Topology has no stream threads and no global threads, \" +\n   375→                                                \"must subscribe to at least one source topic or global table.\");\n   376→            }\n   377→        }\n   378→\n   379→ Consumer<Set<String>> handleTopologyAdditions,\n                                                           final Consumer<Set<String>> handleTopologyRemovals) {\n        try {\n            version.topologyLock.lock();\n            final long latestTopologyVersion = topologyVersion();\n            handleTopologyAdditions.accept(namedTopologiesView());\n            handleTopologyRemovals.accept(namedTopologiesView());\n            threadVersions.put(Thread.currentThread().getName(), latestTopologyVersion);\n        } finally {\n            version.topologyLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void maybeNotifyTopologyVersionListeners() {\n        try {\n            lock();\n            final long minThreadVersion = minimumThreadVersion();\n            final Iterator<TopologyVersionListener> iterator = version.activeTopologyUpdateListeners.listIterator();\n            TopologyVersionListener topologyVersionListener;\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                topologyVersionListener = iterator.next();\n                final long topologyVersionWaitersVersion = topologyVersionListener.topologyVersion;\n                if (minThreadVersion >= topologyVersionWaitersVersion) {\n                    topologyVersionListener.future.complete(null);\n                    iterator.remove();\n                    log.info(\"All threads are now on topology version {}\", topologyVersionListener.topologyVersion);\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Return the minimum version across all live threads, or Long.MAX_VALUE if there are no threads running\n    private long minimumThreadVersion() {\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License. It's assigned to one of the executors for processing.\n * 2. It's locked for committing, removal, other manipulations etc.\n * 3. Neither 1 or 2, i.e. it stays idle. This is possible if we do not have enough executors or because those tasks\n *    are not processable (e.g. because no records fetched) yet.\n */\npublic final class DefaultTaskManager implements TaskManager {\n\n    private final Time time;\n    private final Logger log;\n    private final TasksRegistry tasks;\n\n    private final Lock tasksLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition tasksCondition = tasksLock.newCondition();\n    private final List<TaskId> lockedTasks = new ArrayList<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, StreamsException> uncaughtExceptions = new HashMap<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, TaskExecutor> assignedTasks = new HashMap<>();\n    private final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata;\n\n    private final List<TaskExecutor> taskExecutors;\n\n    public static class DefaultTaskExecutorCreator implements TaskExecutorCreator {\n        @Override\n        public TaskExecutor create(final TaskManager taskManager, final String name, final Time time, final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata) {\n            return new DefaultTaskExecutor(taskManager, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public DefaultTaskManager(final Time time,\n                              final String clientId,\n                              final TasksRegistry tasks,\n                              final TaskExecutorCreator executorCreator,\n                              final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata,\n                              final int numExecutors\n                              ) {\n        final String logPrefix = String.format(\"%s \", clientId);\n        final LogContext logContext = new LogContext(logPrefix);\n        this.log = logContext.logger(DefaultTaskManager.class);\n        this.time = time;\n        this.tasks = tasks;\n        this.taskExecutionMetadata = taskExecutionMetadata;\n\n        this.taskExecutors = new ArrayList<>(numExecutors);\n        for (int i = 1; i <= numExecutors; i++) {\n            final String name = clientId + \"-TaskExecutor-\" + i;\n            this.taskExecutors.add(executorCreator.create(this, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata));\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public StreamTask assignNextTask(final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for getting next task to assign is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            // the most naive scheduling algorithm for now: give the next unlocked, unassigned, and  processable task\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n\n                    assignedTasks.put(task.id(), executor);\n\n                    log.debug(\"Assigned task {} to executor {}\", task.id(), executor.name());\n\n                    return task;\n                }\n            }\n\n            log.debug(\"Found no assignable task for executor {}\", executor.name());\n\n            return null;\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void awaitProcessableTasks(final Supplier<Boolean> isShuttingDown) throws InterruptedException {\n        final boolean interrupted = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await unblocked: returning early from await since a processable task {} was found\", task.id());\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            try {\n                // We re-check the shutdownRequest atomic boolean to avoid a race condition. If this thread was\n                // previously interrupted while awaiting tasksCondition, it is possible to miss the signalAll that\n                // is called during shutdown. If this happens, we end up blocking in the await forever.\n                if (!isShuttingDown.get()) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await blocking\");\n                    tasksCondition.await();\n                } else {\n                    log.debug(\"Not awaiting since shutdown was requested\");\n                }\n            } catch (final InterruptedException ignored) {\n                // we interrupt the thread for shut down and pause.\n                // we can ignore this exception.\n                log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Interrupted while waiting for processable tasks\");\n                return true;\n            }\n            log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Woken up to check for processable tasks\");\n            return false;\n        });\n\n        if (interrupted) {\n            throw new InterruptedException();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void signalTaskExecutors() {\n        log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n        executeWithTasksLocked(tasksCondition::signalAll);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unassignTask(final StreamTask task, final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for unassign task is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            final TaskExecutor lockedExecutor = assignedTasks.get(task.id());\n            if (lockedExecutor == null || lockedExecutor != executor) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Task \" + task.id() + \" is not locked by the executor\");\n            }\n\n            assignedTasks.remove(task.id());\n\n            log.debug(\"Unassigned {} from executor {}\", task.id(), executor.name());\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockTasks(final Set<TaskId> taskIds) {\n        final KafkaFutureImpl<Void> result = new KafkaFutureImpl<>();\n\n        if (taskIds.isEmpty()) {\n            result.complete(null);\n            return result;\n        }\n\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            lockedTasks.addAll(taskIds);\n\n            final Set<TaskId> remainingTaskIds = new ConcurrentSkipListSet<>(taskIds);\n\n            for (final TaskId taskId : taskIds) {\n                final Task task = tasks.initializedTask(taskId);\n\n                if (task == null) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Trying to lock task \" + taskId + \" but it's not owned\");\n                }\n\n                if (!task.isActive()) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The locking task \" + taskId + \" is not an active task\");\n                }\n\n                if (assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                    final TaskExecutor executor = assignedTasks.get(taskId);\n                    log.debug(\"Requesting release of task {} from {}\", taskId, executor.name());\n                    final KafkaFuture<StreamTask> future = executor.unassign();\n                    future.whenComplete((streamTask, throwable) -> {\n                        if (throwable != null) {\n                            result.completeExceptionally(throwable);\n                        } else {\n                            assert !assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId);\n                            // It can happen that the executor handed back the task before we asked it to\n                            // in which case `streamTask` will be null here.\n                            assert streamTask == null || streamTask.id() == taskId;\n                            remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                            if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                                result.complete(null);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    });\n                } else {\n                    remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                    if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                        result.complete(null);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            return result;\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockAllTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() ->\n            lockTasks(tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(Task::id).collect(Collectors.toSet()))\n        );\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unlockTasks(final Set<TaskId> taskIds) {\n\n        if (taskIds.isEmpty()) {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            lockedTasks.removeAll(taskIds);\n            log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unlockAllTasks() {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> unlockTasks(tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(Task::id).collect(Collectors.toSet())));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void add(final Set<StreamTask> tasksToAdd) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasksToAdd) {\n                tasks.addActiveTask(task);\n            }\n            log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Added tasks {} to the task manager to process\", tasksToAdd);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void remove(final TaskId taskId) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is still assigned to executors\");\n            }\n\n            if (!lockedTasks.contains(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not locked yet by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            if (!tasks.containsInitialized(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not owned by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            tasks.removeTask(tasks.initializedTask(taskId));\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Removed task {} from the task manager\", taskId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<ReadOnlyTask> getTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(ReadOnlyTask::new).collect(Collectors.toSet()));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setUncaughtException(final StreamsException exception, final TaskId taskId) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n\n            if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"An uncaught exception can only be set as long as the task is still assigned\");\n            }\n\n            if (uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The uncaught exception must be cleared before restarting processing\");\n            }\n\n            uncaughtExceptions.put(taskId, exception);\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Set an uncaught exception of type {} for task {}, with error message: {}\",\n            exception.getClass().getName(),\n            taskId,\n            exception.getMessage());\n    }\n\n    public Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> drainUncaughtExceptions() {\n        final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> returnValue = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> result = new HashMap<>(uncaughtExceptions);\n            uncaughtExceptions.clear();\n            return result;\n        });\n\n        if (!returnValue.isEmpty()) {\n            log.debug(\"Drained {} uncaught exceptions\", returnValue.size());\n        }\n\n        return returnValue;\n    }\n\n    public boolean hasUncaughtException(final TaskId taskId) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId));\n    }\n\n    private void executeWithTasksLocked(final Runnable action) {\n        tasksLock.lock();\n        try {\n            action.run();\n        } finally {\n            tasksLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private <T> T returnWithTasksLocked(final Supplier<T> action) {\n        tasksLock.lock();\n        try {\n            return action.get();\n        } finally {\n            tasksLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private boolean canProgress(final StreamTask task, final long nowMs) {\n        return\n            taskExecutionMetadata.canProcessTask(task, nowMs) && task.isProcessable(nowMs) ||\n                taskExecutionMetadata.canPunctuateTask(task) && (task.canPunctuateStreamTime() || task.canPunctuateSystemTime());\n    }\n\n    public void startTaskExecutors() {\n        for (final TaskExecutor t: taskExecutors) {\n            t.start();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void shutdown(final Duration duration) {\n        for (final TaskExecutor t: taskExecutors) {\n            t.requestShutdown();\n        }\n        signalTaskExecutors();\n        for (final TaskExecutor t: taskExecutors) {\n            t.awaitShutdown(duration);\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":387,"startLine":1,"totalLines":387}}}

Fetches topology\n * metric snapshots from the metrics backend and manages the transport\n * connection lifecycle. Extends {@link AbstractMetricsTransport} for\n * read/write lock management around the transport.\n */\npublic class StreamsMetricsConnector extends AbstractMetricsTransport {\n\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamsMetricsConnector.class);\n\n    private final MetricsSessionManager sessionManager;\n    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, Long> topologyFetchTimestamps = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n\n    private volatile boolean transportValid = true;\n\n    public StreamsMetricsConnector(final MetricsSessionManager sessionManager) {\n        this.sessionManager = sessionManager;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Fetches the latest metrics for the given topology. Under normal\n     * conditions this acquires a shared (read) lock, which cannot deadlock.\n     * However, when the transport is detected as stale, it falls through to\n     * {@link #refreshTransport()}, which acquires the exclusive (write) lock.\n     *\n     * @param topologyName the name of the topology to fetch metrics for\n     * @return a map of metric name to value\n     */\n    public Map<String, Double> fetchLatestMetrics(final String topologyName) {\n        acquireShared();\n        try {\n            if (isTransportValid()) {\n                // Fast path: transport is healthy, fetch under read lock\n                topologyFetchTimestamps.computeIfAbsent(topologyName, k -> System.currentTimeMillis());\n                return doFetch(topologyName);\n            }\n        } finally {\n            releaseShared();\n        }\n\n        // Slow path: transport is stale, need exclusive access to refresh\n        return refreshTransport(topologyName);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Refreshes the transport connection and then fetches metrics.\n     * Acquires the write lock (exclusive) — this is the A->B edge in\n     * a potential lock ordering issue with the intrinsic monitor.\n     */\n    private Map<String, Double> refreshTransport(final String topologyName) {\n        acquireExclusive();\n        try {\n            log.debug(\"Refreshing stale metrics transport before fetching {}\", topologyName);\n            doDisconnect();\n            doConnect();\n            lastConnectTimeMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n            transportValid = true;\n            return doFetch(topologyName);\n        } finally {\n            releaseExclusive();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Performs periodic transport maintenance. This is called from the\n     * state updater thread (Thread 2). Acquires write lock first, then\n     * validates the session which may acquire the session lock.\n     */\n    public void performMaintenance() {\n        acquireExclusive();\n        try {\n            log.debug(\"Performing metrics transport maintenance\");\n            if (!isTransportValid()) {\n                doDisconnect();\n                doConnect();\n                lastConnectTimeMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n                transportValid = true;\n            }\n            validateSession();\n        } finally {\n            releaseExclusive();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void validateSession() {\n        final MetricsSessionManager.MetricsSession session = sessionManager.currentSession();\n        if (session == null || session.expiryMs <= System.currentTimeMillis()) {\n            log.debug(\"Current metrics session expired, requesting refresh\");\n            sessionManager.refreshSessionIfExpired();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private Map<String, Double> doFetch(final String topologyName) {\n        // In a real implementation this would query the metrics backend\n        topologyFetchTimestamps.put(topologyName, System.currentTimeMillis());\n        return Collections.emptyMap();\n    }\n\n    public void markTransportInvalid() {\n        this.transportValid = false;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doConnect() {\n        log.debug(\"Connecting metrics transport\");\n        transportValid = true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doDisconnect() {\n        log.debug(\"Disconnecting metrics transport\");\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected boolean isTransportValid() {\n        return transportValid;\n    }\n}\n","numLines":144,"startLine":1,"totalLines":144}}}

during rebalancing\n * the shard may change, which triggers listener notifications.\n */\npublic class MetricsSessionManager {\n\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(MetricsSessionManager.class);\n\n    private final ReentrantLock sessionLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition sessionReady = sessionLock.newCondition();\n    private final long sessionTtlMs;\n\n    private volatile MetricsSession currentSession;\n    private boolean rebalancingMode = false;\n\n    private final List<MetricsSessionListener> listeners = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();\n\n    public MetricsSessionManager(final long sessionTtlMs) {\n        this.sessionTtlMs = sessionTtlMs;\n        this.currentSession = new MetricsSession(\n            \"init-\" + ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(10000),\n            0,\n            System.currentTimeMillis() + sessionTtlMs\n        );\n    }\n\n    public void registerListener(final MetricsSessionListener listener) {\n        listeners.add(listener);\n    }\n\n    public void setRebalancingMode(final boolean rebalancing) {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            this.rebalancingMode = rebalancing;\n            log.debug(\"Metrics session manager rebalancing mode set to {}\", rebalancing);\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns the current session. The returned reference is safe to read\n     * without holding the lock due to the volatile field, but the session\n     * may expire at any time.\n     */\n    public MetricsSession currentSession() {\n        return currentSession;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * If the current session has expired, renew it. Called from the transport\n     * maintenance path (Thread 2 in the normal flow).\n     */\n    public void refreshSessionIfExpired() {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            if (currentSession != null && currentSession.expiryMs > System.currentTimeMillis()) {\n                return; // still valid\n            }\n            renewSessionInternal();\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Force a session renewal. Called from the session renewal thread (Thread 3).\n     */\n    public void renewSession() {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            renewSessionInternal();\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void renewSessionInternal() {\n        final MetricsSession oldSession = currentSession;\n        final int newShardId;\n        if (rebalancingMode) {\n            // During rebalancing, the shard assignment may change\n            newShardId = ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(1024);\n        } else {\n            newShardId = oldSession != null ? oldSession.shardId : 0;\n        }\n\n        final MetricsSession newSession = new MetricsSession(\n            \"sess-\" + ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(100000),\n            newShardId,\n            System.currentTimeMillis() + sessionTtlMs\n        );\n        currentSession = newSession;\n        log.debug(\"Renewed metrics session: old={}, new={}\", oldSession, newSession);\n\n        notifyListeners(oldSession, newSession);\n        sessionReady.signalAll();\n    }\n\n    private void notifyListeners(final MetricsSession oldSession, final MetricsSession newSession) {\n        for (final MetricsSessionListener listener : listeners) {\n            try {\n                listener.onSessionChanged(oldSession, newSession);\n            } catch (final Exception e) {\n                log.warn(\"Metrics session listener threw exception\", e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Represents an authenticated metrics session with a token, shard\n     * assignment, and expiry timestamp.\n     */\n    public static class MetricsSession {\n        public final String token;\n        public final int shardId;\n        public final long expiryMs;\n\n        public MetricsSession(final String token, final int shardId, final long expiryMs) {\n            this.token = token;\n            this.shardId = shardId;\n            this.expiryMs = expiryMs;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public String toString() {\n            return \"MetricsSession{token='\" + token + \"', shard=\" + shardId + \", expiry=\" + expiryMs + \"}\";\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":159,"startLine":1,"totalLines":159}}}

final Thread thread2 = new Thread(() -> {\n            connector.performMaintenance();\n        }, \"thread-maintenance\");\n\n        thread1.start();\n        thread2.start();\n\n        thread1.join(5000);\n        thread2.join(5000);\n\n        if (thread1.isAlive() || thread2.isAlive()) {\n            System.err.println(\"DEADLOCK DETECTED: threads did not complete within timeout\");\n            System.exit(1);\n        }\n
